### Round 10: German Grand Prix
*Date: 1983-08-07*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Status | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 15: South African Grand Prix
*Date: 1983-10-15*
